 us vakt deepak kii umr nau saal thi

 It is known that such incidents are common in snake bite cases

 1
 sabase pehle apane sabhi kaamon kii list banaaen

 2

 3
 Never over plan in the circle of finishing work
 ek time par ek hi kaam nipataaen
 It is better to keep meeting continuously, follow what has been decided in the first meeting
 4

 jaise ki mobile main automatic rispos massette on rakhen

 5

 isliye jaruri he ki aap 'na' kahana bhi seekhen

 aisa karne se kaam samay par puraa to hota hi he, saath hi usamen par fections bhi aata he
 6
 aphis main zyaadaatar meeting bina kisi agenda ke hoti he
